 ) Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath has launched the toll-free helpline number 1076 on Thursday
 is helpline ke madhyam se kisi bhi vibhaag se judi samasya ko darj karaayaa ja saktaa he
 Chief Minister Yogi Adityanath said that people from far flung areas will get justice at home through the distance helpline
 siem yogi ne kaha ki is number par sirf shikaayatein darj nahin hongi balki agar ek hafte main samasya kaa nivaaran nahin hua to sambandhit vibhaag ke adhikariyon ke khilaaf karrwai bhi hogi
 With the start of this helpline, complainants will now be able to register their grievances from anywhere in the whole state sitting at home
 helpline number par 24 ghante samasyaayein suni jaaengi
 CM Yogi Adityanath said that the follow-up will go on until the complainant himself says that his problem has been resolved
 shikaayat ke liye 24x7 yani 24 ghante staff maujuud rahegaa
 The Chief Minister said that the government is accountable to the 23 crore people of the state
 ab tak log jaagrukta ke abhaav main ye jaan nahin pate the ki samasya kisko bataaen or kahaan jaaen
 Many times people used to get angry due to non-work by the concerned departments on people's problems
 janata ko sarkari suvidhaon kaa laabh miltaa tha, lekin unhen yah pataa nahin hota tha ki ye suvidhaayen sarkaar ne di hai
 CM Yogi said, the complaint that will come on the helpline will be sent to the concerned department
 ek saptaah ke andar us samasya kaa samaadhaan hoga, agar vibhaag ne karrwai nahin kii to maamla ucch adhikari ko bheja jayega
 Yogi Adityanath said that action will be decided on the officer who does not work
 logon kii samasya par 360 degree par kaam hoga
 Action will also be taken against those making false calls
 mukhyamantri yogi ne kaha ki is helpline kii khaas baat yah he ki isse police or swasthya vibhaag bhi jude rahenge
 The CM helpline call center has a provision of 500 seats, where complaints of people will be heard and recorded 24 hours a week
 itnaa hi nahin, sambandhit vibhaag unase judi shikayaton ke nistaaran or uski monitering bhi karenge
 Yogi Adityanath said that the helpline number has a capacity of 80 thousand inbound calls and 55 thousand outbound calls in a day

 The BJP on Tuesday demanded immediate dismissal of Minister of State for External Affairs Shashi Tharoor on corruption charges and a CBI probe into giving his friend Sunanda Pushkar a 'free stake' of around Rs 75 crore in the Kochi franchise of IPL
 party pravaktaa ravishankar prasad ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, ‘ipel kii kochi frenchiji maamle main tharur ne pratyaksh yaa paroksh laabh ke liye pairvi, sangrakshan or protsaahan dene main apane pad kaa durupyog kiya he, jo bhrashtachar kaa sidhaa maamla banataa he
 He alleged that under the guise of his friend Sunanda Pushkar in this entire case, Tharoor has committed a criminal act by misusing his position and a case is made against him under Section 13 of the anti-corruption Act
 prasad ne kaha ki tharur kise talaak dene ja rahe hai, kisase vivaah karne ja rahe hai yaa pushkar se unke kya rishte hai, inase party kaa koi matlab nahin he
 These are very personal matters of the minister
 khabar he ki tharur apni duusari patni ko talaak dekar pushkar se vivaah karne ja rahe hai
 He said, "the party is however interested in knowing why the Minister of State for External Affairs showed such interest in the Kochi franchise right from the beginning
" How and why did his close friend Pushkar get a free equity of about Rs 75 crore in Kochi franchise without investing money? Prasad said Pushkar, a close friend of the minister, is neither from Kerala nor a big businessman or cricket lover

 But where are we saying this too
 ham to bas yah puch rahe hai ki bina ek paisa liye die is frenchiji main unki mitra pushkar ko 17 pratishat yani 75 karod rupee kii muft hissedari kaise mil gai
 He said, 'it is clear that Shashi Tharoor was given this award under the guise of Pushkar for providing services to Kochi franchise
 in tathyon kaa taarkik arth yahi nikalataa he ki apni kareebi mitra pushkar kii aad main tharur swayan sakriy hai

 The 'aadhaar' card is about to create new records
 aadhaar card sambhavat: duniya kaa sabase bada bieometric identification program he
 The Unique Identification Authority of India (UIDAI) has so far issued around 82 crore cards
 angreji akhbaar da times of india kikhbar ke mutabik, fedral beuro of invastigeshan (FBI) kaa bieometric databes kareeb 15 karod kaa he, jabaki aadhaar card isse kahin zyada ab tak 82 karod logon kaa ban chukaa he
 Till now, the Aadhaar card has been made for about 67 per cent of Indians
 uttar pradesh main UIDAI ne sabase zyada 10 karod 48 lakhaadhar cardjari kiye, jabaki maharashtra main 9 karod or pashchim bengal main 6 karod se zyada logon kaa aadhaar card ban chukaa he

 She was so much aware about the music that no tabla player was taken along quickly for her accompaniment except for one Munna Khan
 unhen maaloom tha ki munne khaan sirf kala dikhaane bhar ke liye hi nahin, na hi gayak kalakaar par chadh jane kii garaj se tabalaa bajaayegaa, balki vah gayika ke saath taan or aalaap ke behad jangal main chupchaap peeche-peeche chalaa aayega
 He will do the same type of work as he does to fill certain amounts of raga-raganis in restrictions
 sangeet ko gaun banaate hue, gayaki ko mukhyadhara main rakhane kaa begum akhtar kaa yah tarika, unhen ek had tak pan
 Mallikarjun ranks in the ranks of veteran artists like Mansoor and Ustad Amir Khan
 in donon murdhanya kalasaadhakon kii gayan-yatra main hamen isi prakaar kaa vichaar samaaya hua miltaa he
 The reason why Begum Akhtar sings to us is as much as 'conceptual singing', the more his clean posture, the careful selection of mid-rhythms, the attention to the correctness of the vocals between the vocals, the less flamboyant than the tabla and the neatness of the three octaves
 Due to the small grainy taunts taken, Gummukt offers him a unique character in the folk of tone and rhythm
 shakeel badayunni kii ghazal ‘i mohabbat tere anjaam pe ronaa aayaa’ begum akhtar kii ghazal adaayagi kaa lagbhag paryaay hi ban gayi he

 unase milane-julne vaale adhikansh logon kaa yahan tak kahana he ki begum ke liye yah ghazal nahin thi, balki unke cancert kaa neshnal antham thi
 Every person who was struck by their affinity - before going to a gathering always used to jokingly tell them that apart from the national anthem, what would you sing today? Or even if Begum Sahiba Mahafil is from Kajri and Dadra, people will not accept it without singing national anthem
 yah ek kalakaar kii apni vidha ke prati atoot siddhahastata kaa ek chota sa pramaan bhar he ki kis tarah kala ke kadradaan us kalakaar dwaara rachi gayi shreshthata ko baar-baar pakadaney kii koshish karte hai
 In this context, an art is the cause of the helplessness of all those in society, in whose companionship is hidden the role of a flare, a satiety, a hope
 begum akhtar bhale hi baar-baar shakeel badayunni kii ghazal gaate hue bahut utsahit yaa prasann hoti hon, magar unhen sunne vaala vyapak shrota samaaj avashya kala kii mayanagari main har baar fasata he, jab-jab ve vahi ek chiz gaati hai

 akhtaribai faizaabadi kaa jo zamana ham aaj silsilewar yaad kar rahe hai, usamen us vakt ke sangeet duniya ke ek rivaaj kii nishandehi karnaa bhi behad zaruri ban jaataa he
 The tawaifs and the left used to decorate the courts in the courts or in their own quarters in two ways - 'siti mahafil' and 'khadi mahafil'
 ‘baithki mehfil’ kaa chalan zyaada tha, kyonki isamen thumari, daadaraa, saadaraa, holi or ghazal aadi kaa bhavpurn pradarshan gayika baithe hue karti thi
 The heavy cloth and dressing of the Biyas used to be the center of attraction of the common people, which is called Peshwaz
 ‘khadi mehfil’ kabhi-kabhaar hi hoti thi, jisamen gaanon kii adaayagi thode ang-sanchaalan ke saath gayika khadey hue karti thi

 sangatiye gayika ke peeche-peeche chalate the, kabhi-kabhaar to daudte bhi the

 tabalanwaazon ke table unke qamar main kase hue aage ko latake rahete the
